***начаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:начаться.html>нача́ться</a> (543)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>нача́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">načátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начаться.html>нача́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">načátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начинаться.html>начина́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to begin, to start, to set in, to break out</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>нача́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">načátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Colloquial pronunciation often puts the stress on the prefix in the past masculine, neuter, and plural, i.e. <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начаться.html>на́чался</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:начаться.html>на́чалось</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:начаться.html>на́чались</a></span>, or on the stem in the past masculine, i.e. <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начаться.html>нача́лся</a></span>.</li></ul>

***начертать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:начертать.html>начерта́ть</a> (19433)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черта.html>черта́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čertá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начертать.html>начерта́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">načertátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to inscribe, to trace</li>
<li>to outline, to delineate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">начерта́тельный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">načertátelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начинать.html>начина́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">načinátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чинить.html>чини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">činítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cause, to administer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

***начислить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:начислить.html>начи́слить</a> (30626)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:числить.html>чи́слить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">číslitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начислить.html>начи́слить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">načíslitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">начисля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">accounting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to charge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:начислить.html>начи́слить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:штраф.html>штраф</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>načíslitʹ</b> štraf</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to levy/impose a fine (on); fine</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">accounting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to credit <i>(to an account)</i>, to credit <i>(an account with)</i>, to post
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:накопленный.html>нако́пленные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:процент.html>проце́нты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> начи́слены</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nakóplennyje procénty ješčó ne načísleny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the interest that has accrued has not been posted yet</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">accounting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to calculate, to reckon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:начислить.html>начи́слить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарплата.html>зарпла́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сотрудник.html>сотру́дникам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдел.html>отде́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>načíslitʹ</b> zarplátu sotrúdnikam otdéla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to draw the payroll for a department</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:начислить.html>начи́слить</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:зарплата.html>зарпла́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>načíslitʹ</b> komú-libo zarplátu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put smb on the payroll</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неверно.html>неве́рно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:начислить.html>начи́слили</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарплата.html>зарпла́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошлый.html>про́шлый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяц</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne nevérno <b>načíslili</b> zarplátu za próšlyj mésjac</i> ― <span class="e-translation">my salary for the past month was miscalculated; last month's payroll had the wrong amount of my salary</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">accounting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to authorize, to assign
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пособие.html>посо́бие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> начи́слено, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выплаченный.html>вы́плачено</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">posóbije býlo načísleno, no ne výplačeno</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the benefit was assigned but not disbursed</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***начистить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:начистить.html>начи́стить</a> (9681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистить.html>чи́стить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čístitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начистить.html>начи́стить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">načístitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">начища́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to polish, to shine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:начистить.html>начи́стить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:физиономия.html>физионо́мию</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:морда.html>мо́рду</a>) кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>načístitʹ</b> fizionómiju (mórdu) komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> to tan smb's hide; trim</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чистый.html>чи́стый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čístyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начисто.html>на́чисто</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">náčisto</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>clean
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переписать.html>переписа́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:начисто.html>на́чисто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">perepisátʹ <b>náčisto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to write/make a clean (new) copy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> outright, decidedly, openly, flatly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:начисто.html>на́чисто</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отказаться.html>отказа́ться</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>náčisto</b> otkazátʹsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to refuse flatly</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:начитанный.html>начи́танный</a> (14352)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начитанный.html>начи́танный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">načítannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">начита́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">načitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начитанный.html>начи́танный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">načítannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>well-read, (of a person) that reads a lot, that has read a lot of books</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:начитаться.html>начита́ться</a> (18489)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">начита́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">načitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:начитаться.html>начита́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">načitátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">начи́тываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to read (any amount of something) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to read a lot</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">начита́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">načitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***наш.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>наш</a> (63)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*našь</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>наш</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naš</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">possessive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> our, ours</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Russian; produced, manufactured <i>etc.</i> in Russia</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>наш</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naš</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>the name of the letter н in the Old Russian alphabet.</li></ol>
